<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">time</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vak.html>vak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">section, compartment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Onomatopoeic.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tikken.html>tikken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tick, to make a ticking sound</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tap</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to type on a typewriter or keyboard</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tag (in a children's game)</li></ol>

***tiller.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a> (87337)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">tilier</i>; equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">till</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tillers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person who tills; a farmer.
<ul><li><b>2000</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alasdair_Gray" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alasdair Gray">Alasdair Gray</a>, <i>The Book of Prefaces</i>, Bloomsbury 2002, page 63:
<dl><dd>In France, Europe's most fertile and cultivated <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>, the <b>tillers</b> of it suffered more and more hunger.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A machine that mechanically tills the soil.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">machine</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">cultivator</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*tilȝer, *telȝer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">telgor</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">telgra</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">telgre</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">"twig, branch, shoot"</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> (also <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">telga</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">telge</i> (whence <span class="Latn" lang="en">tillow</span>)), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*telgô</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*telgǭ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*telguz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twig, branch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*delgʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to split, divide, cut, carve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:telg.html>telg</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">descendant, scion, offshoot, shoot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_Low_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch Low Saxon">Dutch Low Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-nl">telge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twig, branch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zelge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twig, branch, bough</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">telning</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">branch, scion, sapling</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">tág</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">willow-twig</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tillers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A young tree.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Evelyn to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A shoot of a plant which springs from the root or bottom of the original stalk; a sapling; a sucker.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">tillers</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tillering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tillered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To produce new shoots from the root or from around the bottom of the original stalk; stool.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">telier</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beam used in weaving</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">telarium</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tēla</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">web</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tillers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archery</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The stock; a beam on a <a href = vnd.unilang:crossbow.html>crossbow</a> carved to fit the arrow, or the point of balance in a longbow.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1608–1610</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Francis_Beaumont" class="extiw" title="w:Francis Beaumont">Francis Beaumont</a> |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Fletcher_(playwright)" class="extiw" title="w:John Fletcher (playwright)">John <a href = vnd.unilang:fletcher.html>Fletcher</a></a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philaster_(play)" class="extiw" title="w:Philaster (play)">Philaster: Or, Love Lies a Bleeding</a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beaumont_and_Fletcher_folios" class="extiw" title="w:Beaumont and Fletcher folios">Comedies and <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Written by Francis Beavmont and Iohn Fletcher Gentlemen. Never Printed before, and Now Published by the Authours Originall Copies.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite>, London |  Printed for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Humphrey_Robinson" class="extiw" title="w:Humphrey Robinson">Humphrey Robinson</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Three Pidgeons">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, and for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Humphrey_Moseley" class="extiw" title="w:Humphrey Moseley">Humphrey Moseley</a><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Princes Armes in St Pauls Church-yard.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, published 1679, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/3083972">3083972</a></small>, Act 2, scene 2:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>You can shoot in a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a> of iron or wood connected with the rudderhead and leadline, usually forward, in which the rudder <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> moved as desired by the <a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a> (FM 55-501).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The handle of the rudder which the helmsman holds to steer the boat, a piece of wood or metal extending forward from the rudder <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> or through the transom. Generally attached at the top of the rudder.</li>
<li>A handle; a stalk.</li>
<li>The rear-wheel steering control, aboard a <a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:truck.html>truck</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A small drawer; a till.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Dryden to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***timbre.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:timbre.html>timbre</a> (58960)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:timbre.html>timbre</a></i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τύμπανον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">túmpanon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">drum</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tympanum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/timbre" class="extiw" title="w:timbre"><a href = vnd.unilang:timbre.html>timbre</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/timbre" class="extiw" title="w:timbre">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:timbre.html>timbre</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">timbres</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The quality of a sound independent of its pitch and volume.
<ul><li><b>1931</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/H._P._Lovecraft" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:H. P. Lovecraft">H. P. Lovecraft</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Whisperer_in_Darkness" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Whisperer in Darkness">The Whisperer in Darkness</a></i>, chapter 7:
<dl><dd>It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a hard whisper to catch at first, since the grey moustache concealed all movements of the <a href = vnd.unilang:lips.html>lips</a>, and something in its <b><a href = vnd.unilang:timbre.html>timbre</a></b> disturbed <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> greatly; but by concentrating my attention I could soon make out its purport surprisingly well.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>The pitch of a sound as <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> by the ear, described relative to its absolute pitch.
<ul><li><dl><dd>When someone speaks after inhaling helium, their voice <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a <a href = vnd.unilang:higher.html>higher</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:timbre.html>timbre</a></b>. With sulfur hexafluoride, the result <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a lower <b><a href = vnd.unilang:timbre.html>timbre</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The crest on a coat of arms.</li></ol>

***timmer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:timmer.html>timmer</a> (28446)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:timmer.html>timmer</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:timmer.html>timmer</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*timrą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dem-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">build, house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:timmer.html>timmer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:timmer.html>timmers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:timmer.html>timmertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> building, construction</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> construction work</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> room, chamber
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vertrek.html>vertrek</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lokaal.html>lokaal</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> act of building or carpentry</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> building material</li></ol>

***timmeren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:timmeren.html>timmeren</a> (19758)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:timmeren.html>timmeren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">timbren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*timrijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:timmeren.html>timmeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to perform carpentry, to build, to construct</li>
<li>to hammer</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:timmeren.html>timmeren</a></b> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">inergatief</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:houten.html>houten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaken.html>zaken</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:elkaar.html>elkaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zetten.html>zetten</a>

***tine.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tine.html>tine</a> (34627)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:tine.html>tine</a></i>, alteration of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">tinde</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">tind</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">tind</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tindaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:zinnen.html>Zinne</a></i>. Compare also the related <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tind</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tine.html>tine</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tines</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A spike or point on an implement or tool, especially a prong of a fork or a tooth of a comb.
<ul><li><b>1969</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maya_Angelou" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Maya Angelou"><a href = vnd.unilang:maya.html>Maya</a> Angelou</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/I_Know_Why_the_Caged_Bird_Sings" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:I Know Why the Caged Bird Sings">I Know Why the Caged Bird <a href = vnd.unilang:sings.html>Sings</a></a></i>, New York: Bantam, 1971, Chapter 9, pp. 45-46,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/iknowwhycagedbi000maya">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Sitting at the table one day, I <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> the fork in my left hand and pierced a piece of fried chicken. I put the knife through the second <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tine.html>tine</a></b>, as <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> strictly taught, and began to saw against the bone.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A small branch, especially on an antler or horn.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialect</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A wild vetch or tare.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown origin, possibly related to etymology 1.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tine.html>tine</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">tiner</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">tinest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>small, diminutive</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">teen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">affliction</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tine.html>tine</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Trouble; distress; teen.
<ul><li><b>1596</b>, Edmund Spenser, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Faerie_Queene" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Faerie Queene">The Faerie Queene</a></i>:
<dl><dd>As wither'd Weed through cruel Winter's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tine.html>Tine</a></b></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tind</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tine.html>tine</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">tines</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tining</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tined</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To kindle; to set on fire.
<ul><li><b>1700</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Dryden" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Dryden">John Dryden</a>, <i>The First Book of <a href = vnd.unilang:homer.html>Homer</a>'s </i>Ilias:
<dl><dd>The priest with holy hands <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> seen to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tine.html>tine</a></b> / The cloven wood, and pour the ruddy wine.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1596</b>, Edmund Spenser, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Faerie_Queene" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Faerie Queene">The Faerie Queene</a></i>:
<dl><dd>Coals of contention and hot vengeance <b>tin'd</b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To rage; to smart.
<ul><li><b>1596</b>, Edmund Spenser, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Faerie_Queene" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Faerie Queene">The Faerie Queene</a></i>:
<dl><dd>Ne <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> there <a href = vnd.unilang:salve.html>salve</a>, ne <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> there medicine, / That mote recure their wounds; so inly they <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tine.html>tine</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology 5</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">tȳnan</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">tūn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">enclosure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">town</i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tine.html>tine</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">tines</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tining</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tined</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To shut in, or enclose.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Halliwell to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tinka.html>tinka</a> (50518)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tinka.html>tinka</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>  
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:kuur.html>kuur</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gril.html>gril</a>

***tinnitus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tinnitus.html>tinnitus</a> (87331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tinnītus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a jingling, ringing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tinnitus.html>tinnitus</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tinnituses</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The perception of noise, such as a ringing or beating sound, which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> no external source.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***tinsel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tinsel.html>tinsel</a> (87330)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">estincelle</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spark</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">étincelle</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">scintilla</i>; compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">scintillate</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stencil</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tinsel.html>tinsel</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tinsels</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:shining.html>shining</a> material used for ornamental purposes; especially, a very thin, gauzelike cloth with much gold or silver woven into it; also, very thin metal overlaid with a thin coating of gold or silver, brass foil, or the like.
<ul><li><b>1675</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Dryden" class="extiw" title="w:John Dryden">John Dryden</a>, <i>Aureng-zebe</i>
<dl><dd>Who can discern the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tinsel.html>tinsel</a></b> from the gold?</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1963</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Margery_Allingham" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Margery Allingham">Margery Allingham</a>,  “Foreword”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_China_Governess" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The China Governess">The China Governess</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL2004261W">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He stood transfixed before the unaccustomed view of London at night time, a <a href = vnd.unilang:vast.html>vast</a> panorama which reminded him [ | ] of some wood engravings far off and magical, in a printshop in his childhood. They dated from the previous century and <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> coarsely printed on tinted paper, with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tinsel.html>tinsel</a></b> outlining the design.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Very thin <a href = vnd.unilang:strips.html>strips</a> of a glittering, metallic material used as a decoration, and traditionally draped at Christmas time <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> streamers, paper chains and the <a href = vnd.unilang:branches.html>branches</a> of Christmas trees.</li>
<li>Anything <a href = vnd.unilang:shining.html>shining</a> and gaudy; something superficially <a href = vnd.unilang:shining.html>shining</a> and showy, or having a false <a href = vnd.unilang:luster.html>luster</a>, and more pretty than valuable.
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Cowper" class="extiw" title="w:William Cowper">William Cowper</a>:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a> happy peasant! <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a> unhappy bard! His the mere <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tinsel.html>tinsel</a></b>, hers the rich reward.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tinsel.html>tinsel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:tinsel.html>tinsel</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:tinsel.html>tinsel</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Glittering, <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> especially superficially so; gaudy, showy.
<ul><li><b>1590</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edmund_Spenser" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Edmund Spenser">Edmund Spenser</a>, <i>The Faerie Queene</i>, III.1:
<dl><dd>Her garments all <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> wrought of beaten gold, / And all her <a href = vnd.unilang:steed.html>steed</a> with <b>tinsell</b> trappings shone <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tinsel.html>tinsel</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">tinsels</b>, <i>present participle</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">UK</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tinselling</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tinseling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">UK</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tinselled</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tinseled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To adorn with <a href = vnd.unilang:tinsel.html>tinsel</a>; to deck out with cheap but showy ornaments; to make gaudy.
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Pope" class="extiw" title="w:Alexander Pope">Alexander Pope</a>:
<dl><dd>She, <b>tinseled</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> in robes of varying hues</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To give a false sparkle to (something).</li></ol>
</body>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tips.html>tips</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">artsy</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">folksy</i>, and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sudsy</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tiran.html>tiran</a> (10259)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tyrannus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">monarch, ruler; tyrant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τύραννος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">túrannos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tyrant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<p>from <i><a href = vnd.unilang:tl.html>tl</a></i>, an abbreviation of French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tube</i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">luminescent</i>, followed by <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buis.html>buis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tube</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tl-buis.html>tl-buis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="common gender">c</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tl-buis.html>tl-buizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tl-buis.html>tl-buisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tubular fluorescent <a href = vnd.unilang:lamp.html>lamp</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Belgium</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">neonlamp</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">neonbuis</span></li></ul>

***toch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> (91)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></i>, alteration of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doch.html>doch</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>still, nevertheless, anyway
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ziek.html>ziek</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:werkt.html>werkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>He's sick, but he <b>still</b> keeps working.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>after all, despite what <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> expected
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ach.html>Ach</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gekomen.html>gekomen</a>!</i>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a>, you <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> come <b>after all!</b> [I thought you would not.]</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>yes, surely; <span class="use-with-mention">implies a positive contradiction, used to contradict a negative.</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>Wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meekomen.html>meekomen</a>?  |  <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>Toch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a>!</i>
<dl><dd>Don’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> you want to come along?  |  <b>Yes,</b> I do!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">In positive <a href = vnd.unilang:statements.html>statements</a>, a modal particle indicating certainty or emphasis, implying that the speaker considers his statement to be obvious.</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:automonteur.html>automonteur</a>!</i>
<dl><dd>I wouldn’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> know that! I’m no car mechanic!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">In questions, a modal particle indicating uncertainty or sometimes worry, implying that the speaker hopes to be confirmed or reassured; may also be postpositioned as a tag question.</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gekomen.html>gekomen</a>?</i> (with emphasis on <i><a href = vnd.unilang:gekomen.html>gekomen</a></i>)
<dl><dd>He <b><a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a></b> come, <b>didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> he</b>?</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>Jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gerrit.html>Gerrit</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a>?</b></i>
<dl><dd>You’re <a href = vnd.unilang:gerrit.html>Gerrit</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aren.html>aren</a>’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> you?</b></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijwoord.html>Bijwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:gebruikt.html>gebruikt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:extra.html>extra</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:benadrukken.html>benadrukken</a>

<li>in <a href = vnd.unilang:weerwil.html>weerwil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gekomen.html>gekomen</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>

***tocht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tocht.html>tocht</a> (4896)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tocht.html>tocht</a></i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tucht.html>tucht</a></i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tuhtiz</i>, cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:zucht.html>Zucht</a></i>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tijgen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tocht.html>tocht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tochten.html>tochten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tochtje.html>tochtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">march</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">trip</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">draught</span>, air current</li>
<li>A small waterway that connects all the other waterways in a polder to a pump, windmill or sluice.</li></ol>
